--------------------------
-- Text Color Modifiers --
--------------------------

    ~r~ Red        ~g~ Green        ~b~ Blue   
    ~o~ Orange                      ~p~ Purple
    ~y~ Yellow     ~t~ Gray         ~q~ Pink

    ~e~ Enabled    ~s~ Standard     ~l~ SuperDark
    ~d~ Disabled   ~c~ Charcoal     ~u~ SuperDark
    ~h~ Highlight  ~m~ MediumDark   ~v~ SuperDark
    ~n~ Newline    

--------------
-- Mod Type --
--------------
--  Spoilers        - 0
--  Front Bumper    - 1
--  Rear Bumper     - 2
--  Side Skirt      - 3
--  Exhaust         - 4
--  Frame           - 5
--  Grille          - 6
--  Hood            - 7
--  Fender          - 8
--  Right Fender    - 9
--  Roof            - 10
--  Engine          - 11
--  Brakes          - 12
--  Transmission    - 13
--  Horns           - 14 (modIndex from 0 to 51)
--  Suspension      - 15
--  Armor           - 16
--  Front Wheels    - 23
--  Back Wheels     - 24 //only for motocycles
--  Plate holders   - 25
--  Trim Design     - 27
--  Ornaments       - 28
--  Dial Design     - 30
--  Steering Wheel  - 33
--  Shifter Leavers - 34
--  Plaques         - 35
--  Hydraulics      - 38

local cEnums = {}
local floor  = math.floor
local max    = math.max
local min    = math.min

cEnums.player_models = { "player_zero", "player_one", "player_two", }


function cEnums:GET_HASH_KEY(strToHash)
    if not strToHash then return 0 ; end
    local strToHashAsNum = tonumber(strToHash)
    local hash = natives.GAMEPLAY.GET_HASH_KEY(tostring(strToHash))
    if      not hash then return 0
    elseif  hash < 0 then return hash + 0xffffffffff+1
    else    return hash
    end
end

    GetData =
        function(veh,printToTerm,filterPrint)
            if not veh and PLY and PLY.Veh then veh = PLY.Veh ; end
            if not veh then veh = natives.PED.GET_VEHICLE_PED_IS_IN(natives.PLAYER.PLAYER_PED_ID(),false) ; end
            if veh == 0 then return ; end
            local vehData = {}
            local printProvider = echo or print
            natives.VEHICLE.SET_VEHICLE_MOD_KIT(veh, 0)
            for i = 0,#cEnums.vehicles.mods-1 do
                local k = i+1
                local v = cEnums.vehicles.mods[k]
                if ( i < 49 )
                then
                    vehData[i]           = { id = i, max = natives.VEHICLE.GET_NUM_VEHICLE_MODS(veh,i)-1, value = natives.VEHICLE.GET_VEHICLE_MOD(veh,i), name = v, }
                else
                    vehData[i]           = { id = i, max = natives.VEHICLE.DOES_EXTRA_EXIST(veh,i-48),    value = natives.VEHICLE.IS_VEHICLE_EXTRA_TURNED_ON(veh,k-49), name = v, }
                end
                if    printToTerm
                and   ( not filterPrint  or ( type(vehData[i].max) == "number" and vehData[i].max > -1 ) or ( type(vehData[i].max) == "boolean" and vehData[i].max == true ) )
                then  printProvider( string.format( "id= %-3s  max= %-6s  value= %-6s  name= \"%s\",", tostring(vehData[i].id)..",", tostring(vehData[i].max)..",", tostring(vehData[i].value)..",", vehData[i].name ) )
                end
            end
            cEnums.vehicles.vehDataLast = vehData
            return vehData
        end,

    PrintData = function(brief) cEnums.vehicles.GetData(nil,true,brief) ; end,

    SetData =
      function(...)
        local veh = natives.PED.GET_VEHICLE_PED_IS_IN(natives.PLAYER.PLAYER_PED_ID(),false)
        if not veh then veh = 0 ; end
        local inData,dataIndexMax = false,-1
        for k,v in pairs({...}) do if type(v) == "number" and v > 0 then veh = v ; elseif type(v) == "table" then dataIndexMax = #v ; inData = v ; end ; end
        if  veh < 1  or  not natives.ENTITY.IS_ENTITY_A_VEHICLE(veh)  then return ; end
        local vehData = cEnums.vehicles.GetData(veh)
        natives.VEHICLE.SET_VEHICLE_MOD_KIT(veh, 0)
        if not inData or not vehData or #inData == 0 or #inData ~= #vehData then return false ; end
        for i = 0,dataIndexMax,1 do
            if  ( vehData[i] and vehData[i].max and type(vehData[i].max) == "number" and vehData[i].max ~= -1 and inData[i] and type(inData[i].value) ~= "nil" ) then
                if  ( i < 49 )  and  type(inData[i].value) == "number"
                then
                    if      vehData[i].max ~= -1  and inData[i].value >= 0 and inData[i].value <= vehData[i].max
                    then
                        natives.VEHICLE.TOGGLE_VEHICLE_MOD(veh,i,true)
                        print("natives.VEHICLE.SET_VEHICLE_MOD( "..tostring(veh)..", "..tostring(i)..", "..tostring(inData[i].value)..", true ) ")
                        natives.VEHICLE.SET_VEHICLE_MOD( veh, i, inData[i].value, true )
                    end

                elseif  ( type(inData[i].value) == "boolean" and vehData[i].max and natives.VEHICLE.DOES_EXTRA_EXIST(veh,i-48) )
                then
                        print( "natives.VEHICLE.SET_VEHICLE_EXTRA( "..tostring(veh)..", "..tostring(i-48)..", "..tostring(inData[i].value)..")" )
                        natives.VEHICLE.SET_VEHICLE_EXTRA(veh,i-48,inData[i].value)
                end
            end
        end
      end,

    -- vData = cEnums.vehicles.GetData() ; cEnums.vehicles.SetData(vData)

if  natives and natives.PED      and natives.PED.ADD_RELATIONSHIP_GROUP
and natives and natives.GAMEPLAY and natives.GAMEPLAY.GET_HASH_KEY
and natives and natives.PED      and natives.PED.ADD_RELATIONSHIP_GROUP
then

    for k,v in pairs(cEnums.relationship_groups) do
        if type(k) == "number" then
            local curHash = natives.GAMEPLAY.GET_HASH_KEY(v)
            if    curHash < 0 then curHash = curHash + 0xffffffffff + 1 ; end
            if type(curHash) ~= type(k) or curHash ~= k then
                print("WARNING: While loading cEnums.relationship_groups, Hash key mismatch.  Hash given: "..tostring(k).."  Hash actual: "..tostring(curHash))
            -- else
            --     local  c_out = CMemoryBlock(4)
            --     c_out:WriteDWORD32(0,curHash)
            --     natives.PED.ADD_RELATIONSHIP_GROUP(v,c_out)
            --     c_out:Release()
            end
        end
    end
    
end

    BlindFireChance                =  0   ,  [0]   =  "BlindFireChance",
    WeaponShootRateModifier        =  1   ,  [1]   =  "WeaponShootRateModifier",
    TimeBetweenBurstsInCover       =  2   ,  [2]   =  "TimeBetweenBurstsInCover",
    BurstDurationInCover           =  3   ,  [3]   =  "BurstDurationInCover",
    TimeBetweenPeeks               =  4   ,  [4]   =  "TimeBetweenPeeks",
    WeaponAccuracy                 =  5   ,  [5]   =  "WeaponAccuracy",
    FightProficiency               =  6   ,  [6]   =  "FightProficiency",
    StrafeWhenMovingChance         =  7   ,  [7]   =  "StrafeWhenMovingChance",
    WalkWhenStrafingChance         =  8   ,  [8]   =  "WalkWhenStrafingChance",
    AttackWindowDistanceForCover   =  9   ,  [9]   =  "AttackWindowDistanceForCover",
    TimeToInvalidateInjuredTarget  =  10  ,  [10]  =  "TimeToInvalidateInjuredTarget",
    TriggerChargeTime_Near         =  11  ,  [11]  =  "TriggerChargeTime_Near",
    TriggerChargeTime_Far          =  12  ,  [12]  =  "TriggerChargeTime_Far",
    ["Get"] = function(property,ped)        if type(property) == "string" and cEnums.combat_floats[property] then property = cEnums.combat_floats[property] ; elseif type(property) ~= "number" or not cEnums.combat_floats[property] then  return 0 ; end  ;  if not ped then ped = natives.PLAYER.PLAYER_PED_ID() ; end ; return(natives.PED.GET_COMBAT_FLOAT(ped,property) or 0) ; end,
    ["Set"] = function(property,value,ped)  if type(property) == "string" and cEnums.combat_floats[property] then property = cEnums.combat_floats[property] ; elseif type(property) ~= "number" or not cEnums.combat_floats[property] then  return 0 ; end  ;  if not ped then ped = natives.PLAYER.PLAYER_PED_ID() ; end ; if not value then value = cEnums.combat_floats.Get(property,ped) ; end ; natives.PED.SET_COMBAT_FLOAT(ped,property,value) ; return value ; end,
    --[[
      Use like:
      local cur_var = cEnums.combat_floats.Get( "WeaponShootRateModifier", ped )
      cEnums.combat_floats.Set( "WeaponShootRateModifier", cur_var, ped )
    --]]
}

      echo "$VAR" | sed -es,"^",".",g | tr [:upper:] [:lower:]  |  while read -a line ; do [ ${#line[@]} -eq 0 ] && continue ; [ ${#line[@]} -eq 1 ] && curDict=${line[0]:1} && continue ; curSprite=${line[1]} ; printf  "    ${curSprite} = { dict = \"${curDict}\", sprite = \"${curSprite}\", },\n"  ;  done | column -t | sed -es,"^","   ",g

--]]

cEnums.colorsTab = {}

cEnums.colors = setmetatable(
   {   count = 1973, last_input = 0, last_output = {r=0,g=0,b=0}, Clear = function() cEnums.colorsTab = {} ; end, },
   { __index = function(it,ik)
      if type(ik) == "string" then return cEnums.colors[ik] ; end
      local rk = (ik-1)%cEnums.colors.count+1;
      if   cEnums.colorsTab[rk] then return cEnums.colorsTab[rk] ; end
      local targ,oargs = 0,{ r = 0, g = 0, b = 0 };
      if      rk < 3    then oargs.r = 255; oargs.g = 255; oargs.b = 255;
      elseif  rk < 130  then oargs.r = 253 - (rk-3)*2 ; oargs.g = 253 - (rk-3)*2 ; oargs.b = 253 - (rk-3)*2;
      elseif  rk < 132  then
      elseif  rk < 260  then oargs.r = 1+(rk-132)*2;
      elseif  rk < 388  then oargs.g = 1+(rk-260)*2;
      elseif  rk < 516  then oargs.b = 1+(rk-388)*2;
      elseif  rk < 644  then oargs.r = 255              ;  oargs.g =   1+(rk-516) *2  ;
      elseif  rk < 772  then oargs.g = 255              ;  oargs.r = 255-(rk-644) *2  ;
      elseif  rk < 900  then oargs.g = 255              ;  oargs.b =   1+(rk-772) *2  ;
      elseif  rk < 1028 then oargs.b = 255              ;  oargs.g = 255-(rk-900) *2  ;
      elseif  rk < 1156 then oargs.b = 255              ;  oargs.r =   1+(rk-1028)*2  ;
      elseif  rk < 1284 then oargs.r = 255              ;  oargs.b = 255-(rk-1156)*2  ;
      elseif  rk < 1348 then oargs.r = 255              ;  oargs.g = 128-(rk-1284)*2  ;  oargs.b = 128-(rk-1284)*2
      elseif  rk < 1412 then oargs.r = 128-(rk-1348)*2  ;  oargs.g = 255              ;  oargs.b = 128-(rk-1348)*2
      elseif  rk < 1476 then oargs.r = 128-(rk-1412)*2  ;  oargs.g = 128-(rk-1412)*2  ;  oargs.b = 255
      elseif  rk < 1604 then oargs.r = 255              ;  oargs.g = 128-(rk-1476)*2  ;  oargs.b = 128-(rk-1476)
      elseif  rk < 1604 then oargs.r = 255              ;  oargs.g = 255-(rk-1476)*2  ;  oargs.b = 255-(rk-1476)
      elseif  rk < 1732 then oargs.r = 255-(rk-1604)*2  ;  oargs.g = 255              ;  oargs.b = 255-(rk-1604)
      elseif  rk < 1860 then oargs.r = 255-(rk-1732)    ;  oargs.g = 255-(rk-1732)*2  ;  oargs.b = 255
      elseif  rk < 1974 then oargs.r,oargs.g,oargs.b = cEnums.colors_gta[rk-1859].r,cEnums.colors_gta[rk-1859].g,cEnums.colors_gta[rk-1859].b
      end;
      cEnums.colorsTab[rk] = oargs
      return cEnums.colorsTab[rk];
    end
  }
)

--[[  Above this is a fully mathmatical/metatable conversion of this solution.

cEnums.colorsTab = {
     [1]  = { 255, 255,  1, "r","g","b", }, --     1 to 1
     [2]  = { 255, 255,  1, "r","g","b", }, --     2 to 2
     [3]  = { 253,   1, -2, "r","g","b", }, --     3 to 129
   [130]  = {   0,   0,  1, "r","g","b", }, --   130 to 130
   [131]  = {   0,   0,  1, "r","g","b", }, --   131 to 131
   [132]  = {   1, 255,  2, "r",         }, --   132 to 259
   [260]  = {   1, 255,  2, "g",         }, --   260 to 387
   [388]  = {   1, 255,  2, "b",         }, --   388 to 515
   [516]  = {   1, 255,  2, "R","g",     }, --   516 to 643
   [644]  = { 255,   1, -2, "G","r",     }, --   644 to 771
   [772]  = {   1, 255,  2, "G","b",     }, --   772 to 899
   [900]  = { 255,   1, -2, "B","g",     }, --   900 to 1027
  [1028]  = {   1, 255,  2, "B","r",     }, --  1028 to 1155
  [1156]  = { 255,   1, -2, "R","b",     }, --  1156 to 1283
}

local  tcount = 0 ; for k,v in pairs(cEnums.colorsTab) do for i = v[1],v[2],v[3] do tcount = tcount + 1 ;end ;end

cEnums.colors = setmetatable(
   { count = tcount, },
   { __index = function(it,ik)
      local rk = (ik-1)%cEnums.colors.count+1
      local targ,oargs = 0,{ r = 0, g = 0, b = 0 }
      for k,v in pairs(cEnums.colorsTab) do if k > targ and rk >= k then targ = k ; end ; end
      local count = targ
      for i = cEnums.colorsTab[targ][1],cEnums.colorsTab[targ][2],cEnums.colorsTab[targ][3] do
        if rk == count then
          local j = 1
          while j < 4 do
            if cEnums.colorsTab[targ][j+3] then
              local v,vlower = cEnums.colorsTab[targ][j+3],string.lower(cEnums.colorsTab[targ][j+3])
              if oargs[vlower] and vlower == v then
                oargs[vlower] = i
              elseif oargs[vlower] then
                oargs[vlower] = 255
              end
            end
            j=j+1
          end
        end
        count = count + 1
      end
      return oargs
    end
  }
)
--]]

--[[ Above this block is a metatable replacement for cEnums.colors
cEnums.colors2 = {}
local c = cEnums.colors2
--]]
--[[ White                                 ]] -- c[#c+1] = { r = 255, g = 255, b = 255 }
--[[ White                                 ]] -- c[#c+1] = { r = 255, g = 255, b = 255 }
--[[ Grey scale, from 253 to 1 , by -2's   ]] -- for i =   253,  1,    -2 do c[#c+1] = { r = i,  g = i,  b = i, } ; end
--[[ Black                                 ]] -- c[#c+1] = { r = 0,   g = 0,   b = 0   }
--[[ Black                                 ]] -- c[#c+1] = { r = 0,   g = 0,   b = 0   }
--[[ From 256  to 4.0,  by  4's, Red       ]] -- for i =   1.0,  255,   2  do  c[#c+1] = { r =       i,         g =       0,          b =       0,         } ; end
--[[ From 256  to 4.0,  by -4's, Green     ]] -- for i =   1.0,  255,   2  do  c[#c+1] = { r =       0,         g =       i,          b =       0,         } ; end
--[[ From 256  to 4.0,  by  4's, Blue      ]] -- for i =   1.0,  255,   2  do  c[#c+1] = { r =       0,         g =       0,          b =       i,         } ; end
--[[ From 4.25 to 255,  by  4's, Rg        ]] -- for i =   1.0,  255,   2  do  c[#c+1] = { r =      255,        g =       i,          b =       0,         } ; end
--[[ From 255  to 4.25, by  4's, Gr        ]] -- for i =   255,    1,  -2  do  c[#c+1] = { r =       i,         g =      255,         b =       0,         } ; end
--[[ From 4.25 to 255,  by  4's, Gb        ]] -- for i =   1.0,  255,   2  do  c[#c+1] = { r =       0,         g =      255,         b =       i,         } ; end
--[[ From 255  to 4.25, by  4's, Bg        ]] -- for i =   255,    1,  -2  do  c[#c+1] = { r =       0,         g =       i,          b =      255,        } ; end
--[[ From 4.25 to 255,  by  4's, Br        ]] -- for i =   1.0,  255,   2  do  c[#c+1] = { r =       i,         g =       0,          b =      255,        } ; end
--[[ From 255  to 4.25, by  4's, Rb        ]] -- for i =   255,    1,  -2  do  c[#c+1] = { r =      255,        g =       0,          b =       i,         } ; end

--[[

# Bash script for converting bmp to txt, then txt to lua x/y format.

in_image=/var/tmp/8-bit-15x15-smile.bmp
bmp_info "${in_image}" ; tail -c $(( BMP_DATA_SIZE )) "${in_image}" | bin2hex -w0 | sed -es,".\{$(( BMP_BPP * ( BMP_WIDTH + BMP_PAD ) * 2 ))\}","&\n",g | sed -es,".\{$(( BMP_PAD*2 ))\}$",,g  -es,".\{$(( BMP_BPP * 2 ))\}"," &",g | tac \
\
|(
  while read -a line ; do for i in ${!line[@]} ; do echo -n " ${line[${#line[@]}-i]}" ; done ; echo "" ; done
 ) \
\
|(
  lineNum=0
  charNum=0
  ignoreValue=( ff )
  operation='echo -n "{x=${charNum},y=${lineNum}}, "'
  while read -a line
  do
        lineNum=$(( lineNum + 1 ))
        charNum=0
        for c in ${line[@]}
        do
             charNum=$(( charNum + 1 ))
             [ "${c}" != "${ignoreValue}" ] && eval "${operation}"
             
        done
        
  done
  echo ""
 )

--]]

cEnums.camDistMod = { [0] = 1, [1] = 3, [2] = 5, [3] = 5, [4] = 0, }

cEnums.tintList = {0, 1 ,2 ,3 ,4 ,5 ,6 ,7}

for k,v in pairs(cEnums.weapons) do
    if ( type(k) == "string" )
    then  cEnums.weapons[v] = k
    end
end

if  natives and natives.GAMEPLAY and natives.GAMEPLAY.GET_HASH_KEY
then
    for k,v in ipairs(cEnums.weapons) do
        local curHash = natives.GAMEPLAY.GET_HASH_KEY(v)
        if curHash < 0 then curHash = curHash + 0xffffffffff + 1 ; end
        cEnums.weapons[curHash] = cEnums.weapons[k]
        cEnums.weapons[v]       = curHash
    end

    for k,v in pairs(cEnums.weapons) do
        if ( type(k) == "number" )
        then
            if  ( k > 0 ) and ( k < 1000 ) then  local hash = natives.GAMEPLAY.GET_HASH_KEY(v) ; if hash < 0 then hash = hash + 0xffffffffff + 1 ; end ; cEnums.weapons[hash] = v
                                           else  cEnums.weapons[v] = k
            end
        end
    end

    for k = 1,#cEnums.player_models do
        local v    = cEnums.player_models[k]
        local hash = natives.GAMEPLAY.GET_HASH_KEY(v)
        if hash < 0 then curHash = hash + 0xffffffffff + 1 ; end
        cEnums.player_models[hash] = v
        cEnums.player_models[v]    = hash
    end

end

table.sort(cEnums.scenarios)

return cEnums
